\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Gets a CUDA array plane from a CUDA array. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga598b46f4b973520bbb04aeadaab0560d}{cu\+Array\+Destroy}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} h\+Array)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Destroys a CUDA array. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga96aa0d157943c9290cc04aef10824e0c}{cu\+Array3\+DCreate}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{p\+Handle}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{p\+Allocate\+Array}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Creates a 3D CUDA array. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Get a 3D CUDA array descriptor. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga2194e4f8117e242cc371ded1abb054e4}{cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Create}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{p\+Handle}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{p\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Desc}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{num\+Mipmap\+Levels}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Creates a CUDA mipmapped array. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gaff70c3a8c820c60af579c638771038e9}{cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Level}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{p\+Level\+Array}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}} h\+Mipmapped\+Array, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} level)

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+MANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ memory management functions of the low-\/level CUDA driver API (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+) \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+ENDMANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+

This section describes the memory management functions of the low-\/level CUDA driver application programming interface. 

\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga96aa0d157943c9290cc04aef10824e0c}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga96aa0d157943c9290cc04aef10824e0c} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuArray3DCreate@{cuArray3DCreate}}
\index{cuArray3DCreate@{cuArray3DCreate}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArray3DCreate()}{cuArray3DCreate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array3\+DCreate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Allocate\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a 3D CUDA array. 

Creates a CUDA array according to the CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR structure {\ttfamily p\+Allocate\+Array} and returns a handle to the new CUDA array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Handle}. The CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR is defined as\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Depth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}}\ Format;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NumChannels;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Flags;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\_ARRAY3D\_DESCRIPTOR}};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Width}, {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} are the width, height, and depth of the CUDA array (in elements); the following types of CUDA arrays can be allocated\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A 1D array is allocated if {\ttfamily Height} and {\ttfamily Depth} extents are both zero.
\item A 2D array is allocated if only {\ttfamily Depth} extent is zero.
\item A 3D array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero.
\item A 1D layered CUDA array is allocated if only {\ttfamily Height} is zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is set. Each layer is a 1D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A 2D layered CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is set. Each layer is a 2D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A cubemap CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} flag is set. {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be six. A cubemap is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array, where the six layers represent the six faces of a cube. The order of the six layers in memory is the same as that listed in \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3df6d8bbf8f19ba6956c87c6b8f8eb86}{CUarray\+\_\+cubemap\+\_\+face}.
\item A cubemap layered CUDA array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero, and both, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flags are set. {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be a multiple of six. A cubemap layered CUDA array is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array that consists of a collection of cubemaps. The first six layers represent the first cubemap, the next six layers form the second cubemap, and so on.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Format specifies the format of the elements; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\+\_\+format} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7}{CUarray\_format\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ae0af5f5a0ffa8e16a5c720364ccd5dac}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ad0f11e851e891af6f204cf05503ba525}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a52b891ad5d4080db0fb2e23fe71614a0}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a376b799ee12ce9e1de0c34cfa7839284}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x08,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a80864598b1579bd90fab79369072478f}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x09,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a6db055c31d053bd1d5ebbaa98de2bad3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x0a,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a95c97289b540ff36334722ec745f53a3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_HALF}}\ =\ 0x10,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a8140f3b0de3d87bdbf26964c24840f3c}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_FLOAT}}\ =\ 0x20}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Num\+Channels} specifies the number of packed components per CUDA array element; it may be 1, 2, or 4;
\item \+::\+Flags may be set to
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} to enable creation of layered CUDA arrays. If this flag is set, {\ttfamily Depth} specifies the number of layers, not the depth of a 3D array.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7287c43cacf1ed05865d6bcad1a23cd9}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+SURFACE\+\_\+\+LDST} to enable surface references to be bound to the CUDA array. If this flag is not set, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_u_r_f_r_e_f___d_e_p_r_e_c_a_t_e_d_ga98601aa76ddd3cedd3072207de066fc6}{cu\+Surf\+Ref\+Set\+Array} will fail when attempting to bind the CUDA array to a surface reference.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} to enable creation of cubemaps. If this flag is set, {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be six. If the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is also set, then {\ttfamily Depth} must be a multiple of six.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga0c929c92a91f4d9f9f49bae0131a6ccf}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+TEXTURE\+\_\+\+GATHER} to indicate that the CUDA array will be used for texture gather. Texture gather can only be performed on 2D CUDA arrays.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily Width}, {\ttfamily Height} and {\ttfamily Depth} must meet certain size requirements as listed in the following table. All values are specified in elements. Note that for brevity\textquotesingle{}s sake, the full name of the device attribute is not specified. For ex., TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH refers to the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa1f7318312b520cd5bc19eb97659e8215}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAXIMUM\+\_\+\+TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH}.

Note that 2D CUDA arrays have different size requirements if the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga0c929c92a91f4d9f9f49bae0131a6ccf}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+TEXTURE\+\_\+\+GATHER} flag is set. {\ttfamily Width} and {\ttfamily Height} must not be greater than \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aaa3d02a5e777b952280c1f8b4fac477ef}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAXIMUM\+\_\+\+TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+GATHER\+\_\+\+WIDTH} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa9ceeac801dbf34671de63cc7ca383935}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAXIMUM\+\_\+\+TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+GATHER\+\_\+\+HEIGHT} respectively, in that case.

\tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{3}{|X[-1]}|}

\{(width range in elements), (height range), (depth range)\}}} &{\bfseries{Valid extents with CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+SURFACE\+\_\+\+LDST set~\newline
 \{(width range in elements), (height range), (depth range)\}}} \\\cline{1-3}
1D &
\footnotesize \{ (1,TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH), 0, 0 \}
\normalsize  &
\footnotesize \{ (1,SURFACE1\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH), 0, 0 \}
\normalsize  \\\cline{1-3}
2D &
\footnotesize \{ (1,TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+HEIGHT), 0 \}
\normalsize  &
\footnotesize \{ (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+HEIGHT), 0 \}
\normalsize  \\\cline{1-3}

\normalsize  &

\footnotesize \{ (1,TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+WIDTH), 0, (1,TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+LAYERS) \}
\normalsize  &
\footnotesize \{ (1,SURFACE1\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+WIDTH), 0, (1,SURFACE1\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+LAYERS) \}
\normalsize  \\\cline{1-3}
2D Layered &
\footnotesize \{ (1,TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+HEIGHT), (1,TEXTURE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+LAYERS) \}
\normalsize  &
\footnotesize \{ (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+HEIGHT), (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED\+\_\+\+LAYERS) \}
\normalsize  \\\cline{1-3}
Cubemap &
\footnotesize \{ (1,TEXTURECUBEMAP\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,TEXTURECUBEMAP\+\_\+\+WIDTH), 6 \}
\normalsize  &

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArray3DGetDescriptor()}{cuArray3DGetDescriptor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array3\+DGet\+Descriptor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Array\+Descriptor,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{h\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get a 3D CUDA array descriptor. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Array\+Descriptor} a descriptor containing information on the format and dimensions of the CUDA array {\ttfamily h\+Array}. It is useful for subroutines that have been passed a CUDA array, but need to know the CUDA array parameters for validation or other purposes.

This function may be called on 1D and 2D arrays, in which case the {\ttfamily Height} and/or {\ttfamily Depth} members of the descriptor struct will be set to 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Array\+Descriptor} & -\/ Returned 3D array descriptor \\
\hline
{\em h\+Array} & -\/ 3D array to get descriptor of\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab27ac43f7ce8446f5c9636dd73fb2139}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+CONTEXT\+\_\+\+IS\+\_\+\+DESTROYED} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArrayCreate()}{cuArrayCreate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array\+Create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Allocate\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a 1D or 2D CUDA array. 

Creates a CUDA array according to the CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR structure {\ttfamily p\+Allocate\+Array} and returns a handle to the new CUDA array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Handle}. The CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR is defined as\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}}\ Format;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NumChannels;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\_ARRAY\_DESCRIPTOR}};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Width}, and {\ttfamily Height} are the width, and height of the CUDA array (in elements); the CUDA array is one-\/dimensional if height is 0, two-\/dimensional otherwise;
\item \+::\+Format specifies the format of the elements; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\+\_\+format} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7}{CUarray\_format\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ae0af5f5a0ffa8e16a5c720364ccd5dac}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ad0f11e851e891af6f204cf05503ba525}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a52b891ad5d4080db0fb2e23fe71614a0}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a376b799ee12ce9e1de0c34cfa7839284}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x08,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a80864598b1579bd90fab79369072478f}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x09,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a6db055c31d053bd1d5ebbaa98de2bad3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x0a,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a95c97289b540ff36334722ec745f53a3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_HALF}}\ =\ 0x10,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a8140f3b0de3d87bdbf26964c24840f3c}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_FLOAT}}\ =\ 0x20}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Num\+Channels} specifies the number of packed components per CUDA array element; it may be 1, 2, or 4;
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArrayGetDescriptor()}{cuArrayGetDescriptor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array\+Get\+Descriptor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Array\+Descriptor,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{h\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get a 1D or 2D CUDA array descriptor. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Array\+Descriptor} a descriptor containing information on the format and dimensions of the CUDA array {\ttfamily h\+Array}. It is useful for subroutines that have been passed a CUDA array, but need to know the CUDA array parameters for validation or other purposes.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}{cuArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array\+Get\+Memory\+Requirements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memory\+Requirements,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA array. 

Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA array in {\ttfamily memory\+Requirements} If the CUDA array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga854c29dbc47d04a4e42863cb87487d55}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DEFERRED\+\_\+\+MAPPING} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned.

The returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st_a19921be32de612b22f898a6fd24ebb73}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS\+::size} represents the total size of the CUDA array. The returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st_afc64d15c6b760c6346b2d837dd3bfe51}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS\+::alignment} represents the alignment necessary for mapping the CUDA array.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuArrayGetPlane@{cuArrayGetPlane}}
\index{cuArrayGetPlane@{cuArrayGetPlane}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArrayGetPlane()}{cuArrayGetPlane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array\+Get\+Plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Plane\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{h\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{plane\+Idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a CUDA array plane from a CUDA array. 

Returns in {\ttfamily p\+Plane\+Array} a CUDA array that represents a single format plane of the CUDA array {\ttfamily h\+Array}.

If {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} is greater than the maximum number of planes in this array or if the array does not have a multi-\/planar format e.\+g\+: \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a64889c93ccc518395eb985203735d40c}{CU\+\_\+\+AD\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+NV12}, then \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} is returned.

Note that if the {\ttfamily h\+Array} has format \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a64889c93ccc518395eb985203735d40c}{CU\+\_\+\+AD\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+NV12}, then passing in 0 for {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} returns a CUDA array of the same size as {\ttfamily h\+Array} but with one channel and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ae0af5f5a0ffa8e16a5c720364ccd5dac}{CU\+\_\+\+AD\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+UNSIGNED\+\_\+\+INT8} as its format. If 1 is passed for {\ttfamily plane\+Idx}, then the returned CUDA array has half the height and width of {\ttfamily h\+Array} with two channels and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ae0af5f5a0ffa8e16a5c720364ccd5dac}{CU\+\_\+\+AD\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+UNSIGNED\+\_\+\+INT8} as its format.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Plane\+Array} & -\/ Returned CUDA array referenced by the {\ttfamily plane\+Idx} \\
\hline
{\em h\+Array} & -\/ Multiplanar CUDA array \\
\hline
{\em plane\+Idx} & -\/ Plane index\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuArrayGetSparseProperties()}{cuArrayGetSparseProperties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{sparse\+Properties,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA array. 

Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA array in {\ttfamily sparse\+Properties} If the CUDA array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga8e13c9d3ef98d1f3dce95901a115abc2}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+SPARSE} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned.

If the returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a4b165566317bb2212ef61b5904323e11}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::flags} contains \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga0dcf4ba7e64caa5c1aa4e88caa7f659a}{CU\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+\_\+\+SINGLE\+\_\+\+MIPTAIL}, then \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a632ab9d5ee6722ef8e81c04a9a58dcdd}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+Size} represents the total size of the array. Otherwise, it will be zero. Also, the returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_af3ed467c8e045c2a0c71c45154621680}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+First\+Level} is always zero. Note that the {\ttfamily array} must have been allocated using cu\+Array\+Create or cu\+Array3\+DCreate. For CUDA arrays obtained using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gaff70c3a8c820c60af579c638771038e9}{cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Level}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned. Instead, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga44e401fb3c212fd9d2eb3b9f9370f3d8}{cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties} must be used to obtain the sparse properties of the entire CUDA mipmapped array to which {\ttfamily array} belongs to.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em sparse\+Properties} & -\/ Pointer to CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em array} & -\/ CUDA array to get the sparse properties of \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuIpcCloseMemHandle()}{cuIpcCloseMemHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Ipc\+Close\+Mem\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Attempts to close memory mapped with cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle. 

Decrements the reference count of the memory returned by cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle by 1. When the reference count reaches 0, this API unmaps the memory. The original allocation in the exporting process as well as imported mappings in other processes will be unaffected.

Any resources used to enable peer access will be freed if this is the last mapping using them.

IPC functionality is restricted to devices with support for unified addressing on Linux and Windows operating systems. IPC functionality on Windows is restricted to GPUs in TCC mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dptr} & -\/ Device pointer returned by cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab9a95891afee8e479ca2e89595b51a2f}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+MAP\+\_\+\+FAILED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuIpcGetEventHandle@{cuIpcGetEventHandle}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuIpcGetEventHandle()}{cuIpcGetEventHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Event\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_uipc_event_handle__st}{CUipc\+Event\+Handle}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets an interprocess handle for a previously allocated event. 

Takes as input a previously allocated event. This event must have been created with the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga58fed1f4772abb4551d21d44dfcb892caadab662356d24cf59f3d7de07c3cd52e}{CU\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+INTERPROCESS} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga58fed1f4772abb4551d21d44dfcb892cadaa5463f64794c10b78c603d23c0bff2}{CU\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+DISABLE\+\_\+\+TIMING} flags set. This opaque handle may be copied into other processes and opened with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gae6c9cb28c5d6548bbd70a6e474a1ce10}{cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Event\+Handle} to allow efficient hardware synchronization between GPU work in different processes.

After the event has been opened in the importing process, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga8b5c6177fdc919e456a73684a01d2bac}{cu\+Event\+Record}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga7b793010359bac523d837b3f8c81f2c5}{cu\+Event\+Synchronize}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_t_r_e_a_m_gad09bc2964bf3441c02bfe22c346f73e5}{cu\+Stream\+Wait\+Event} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga862b4b51fb9fa95371a83c722d10fbc8}{cu\+Event\+Query} may be used in either process. Performing operations on the imported event after the exported event has been freed with cu\+Event\+Destroy will result in undefined behavior.

IPC functionality is restricted to devices with support for unified addressing on Linux and Windows operating systems. IPC functionality on Windows is restricted to GPUs in TCC mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Handle} & -\/ Pointer to a user allocated CUipc\+Event\+Handle in which to return the opaque event handle \\
\hline
{\em event} & -\/ Event allocated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga58fed1f4772abb4551d21d44dfcb892caadab662356d24cf59f3d7de07c3cd52e}{CU\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+INTERPROCESS} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga58fed1f4772abb4551d21d44dfcb892cadaa5463f64794c10b78c603d23c0bff2}{CU\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+DISABLE\+\_\+\+TIMING} flags.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab9a95891afee8e479ca2e89595b51a2f}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+MAP\+\_\+\+FAILED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga092829e272a04c7ad1b4d05bdecaa4b8}{cu\+Event\+Create}, cu\+Event\+Destroy, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga7b793010359bac523d837b3f8c81f2c5}{cu\+Event\+Synchronize}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga862b4b51fb9fa95371a83c722d10fbc8}{cu\+Event\+Query}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_t_r_e_a_m_gad09bc2964bf3441c02bfe22c346f73e5}{cu\+Stream\+Wait\+Event}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gae6c9cb28c5d6548bbd70a6e474a1ce10}{cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Event\+Handle}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga45c5b093d37f7d49effe18d315f61642}{cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Mem\+Handle}, cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga19c47400769323c67b5f807b9d482742}{cu\+Ipc\+Close\+Mem\+Handle}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_gafff40bb17a5e0a96b513fc2bd60dd4f9}{cuda\+Ipc\+Get\+Event\+Handle}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga45c5b093d37f7d49effe18d315f61642}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga45c5b093d37f7d49effe18d315f61642} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuIpcGetMemHandle@{cuIpcGetMemHandle}}
\index{cuIpcGetMemHandle@{cuIpcGetMemHandle}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuIpcGetMemHandle()}{cuIpcGetMemHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Mem\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_uipc_mem_handle__st}{CUipc\+Mem\+Handle}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets an interprocess memory handle for an existing device memory allocation. 

Takes a pointer to the base of an existing device memory allocation created with cu\+Mem\+Alloc and exports it for use in another process. This is a lightweight operation and may be called multiple times on an allocation without adverse effects.

If a region of memory is freed with cu\+Mem\+Free and a subsequent call to cu\+Mem\+Alloc returns memory with the same device address, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga45c5b093d37f7d49effe18d315f61642}{cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Mem\+Handle} will return a unique handle for the new memory.

IPC functionality is restricted to devices with support for unified addressing on Linux and Windows operating systems. IPC functionality on Windows is restricted to GPUs in TCC mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Handle} & -\/ Pointer to user allocated CUipc\+Mem\+Handle to return the handle in. \\
\hline
{\em dptr} & -\/ Base pointer to previously allocated device memory\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab9a95891afee8e479ca2e89595b51a2f}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+MAP\+\_\+\+FAILED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
cu\+Mem\+Alloc, cu\+Mem\+Free, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gafb5982c0e44b70fcc81c209d8921fdaa}{cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Event\+Handle}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gae6c9cb28c5d6548bbd70a6e474a1ce10}{cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Event\+Handle}, cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga19c47400769323c67b5f807b9d482742}{cu\+Ipc\+Close\+Mem\+Handle}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___d_e_v_i_c_e_ga13ea0fd02681361d2676bffdce7f48dc}{cuda\+Ipc\+Get\+Mem\+Handle} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuIpcOpenEventHandle@{cuIpcOpenEventHandle}}
\index{cuIpcOpenEventHandle@{cuIpcOpenEventHandle}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuIpcOpenEventHandle()}{cuIpcOpenEventHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Event\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Event,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_uipc_event_handle__st}{CUipc\+Event\+Handle}}}]{handle }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Opens an interprocess event handle for use in the current process. 

Opens an interprocess event handle exported from another process with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gafb5982c0e44b70fcc81c209d8921fdaa}{cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Event\+Handle}. This function returns a \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent} that behaves like a locally created event with the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga58fed1f4772abb4551d21d44dfcb892cadaa5463f64794c10b78c603d23c0bff2}{CU\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+DISABLE\+\_\+\+TIMING} flag specified. This event must be freed with cu\+Event\+Destroy.

Performing operations on the imported event after the exported event has been freed with cu\+Event\+Destroy will result in undefined behavior.

IPC functionality is restricted to devices with support for unified addressing on Linux and Windows operating systems. IPC functionality on Windows is restricted to GPUs in TCC mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Event} & -\/ Returns the imported event \\
\hline
{\em handle} & -\/ Interprocess handle to open\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab9a95891afee8e479ca2e89595b51a2f}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+MAP\+\_\+\+FAILED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaad60abcaa3f2710f961db8c383bb95cae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+PEER\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+UNSUPPORTED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga2589074587a0a18e154e3754dbcd356a}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga2589074587a0a18e154e3754dbcd356a} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuIpcOpenMemHandle@{cuIpcOpenMemHandle}}
\index{cuIpcOpenMemHandle@{cuIpcOpenMemHandle}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuIpcOpenMemHandle()}{cuIpcOpenMemHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pdptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_uipc_mem_handle__st}{CUipc\+Mem\+Handle}}}]{handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Opens an interprocess memory handle exported from another process and returns a device pointer usable in the local process. 

Maps memory exported from another process with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga45c5b093d37f7d49effe18d315f61642}{cu\+Ipc\+Get\+Mem\+Handle} into the current device address space. For contexts on different devices cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle can attempt to enable peer access between the devices as if the user called \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___p_e_e_r___a_c_c_e_s_s_ga09abdb12526cbcacece926887a76a5e6}{cu\+Ctx\+Enable\+Peer\+Access}. This behavior is controlled by the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga6c0df18fa0028ed4677da152bc4f5eeea567565e36fc87a2180109170a0501947}{CU\+\_\+\+IPC\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+LAZY\+\_\+\+ENABLE\+\_\+\+PEER\+\_\+\+ACCESS} flag. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___p_e_e_r___a_c_c_e_s_s_gadd7611b1357104d94a8d49d16df2e08f}{cu\+Device\+Can\+Access\+Peer} can determine if a mapping is possible.

Contexts that may open \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUipc\+Mem\+Handles} are restricted in the following way. \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUipc\+Mem\+Handles} from each \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice} in a given process may only be opened by one \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext} per \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice} per other process.

If the memory handle has already been opened by the current context, the reference count on the handle is incremented by 1 and the existing device pointer is returned.

Memory returned from cu\+Ipc\+Open\+Mem\+Handle must be freed with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga19c47400769323c67b5f807b9d482742}{cu\+Ipc\+Close\+Mem\+Handle}.

Calling cu\+Mem\+Free on an exported memory region before calling \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga19c47400769323c67b5f807b9d482742}{cu\+Ipc\+Close\+Mem\+Handle} in the importing context will result in undefined behavior.

IPC functionality is restricted to devices with support for unified addressing on Linux and Windows operating systems. IPC functionality on Windows is restricted to GPUs in TCC mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pdptr} & -\/ Returned device pointer \\
\hline
{\em handle} & -\/ CUipc\+Mem\+Handle to open \\
\hline
{\em Flags} & -\/ Flags for this operation. Must be specified as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga6c0df18fa0028ed4677da152bc4f5eeea567565e36fc87a2180109170a0501947}{CU\+\_\+\+IPC\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+LAZY\+\_\+\+ENABLE\+\_\+\+PEER\+\_\+\+ACCESS}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaab9a95891afee8e479ca2e89595b51a2f}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+MAP\+\_\+\+FAILED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa168ef870793a31ef4cdd7cb6e279b34a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+MANY\+\_\+\+PEERS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
No guarantees are made about the address returned in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pdptr}. In particular, multiple processes may not receive the same address for the same {\ttfamily handle}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemAlloc()}{cuMemAlloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Alloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{bytesize }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocates device memory. 

Allocates {\ttfamily bytesize} bytes of linear memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. The allocated memory is suitably aligned for any kind of variable. The memory is not cleared. If {\ttfamily bytesize} is 0, cu\+Mem\+Alloc() returns \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dptr} & -\/ Returned device pointer \\
\hline
{\em bytesize} & -\/ Requested allocation size in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemAllocHost()}{cuMemAllocHost()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Host (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{bytesize }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocates page-\/locked host memory. 

Allocates {\ttfamily bytesize} bytes of host memory that is page-\/locked and accessible to the device. The driver tracks the virtual memory ranges allocated with this function and automatically accelerates calls to functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga80d68f9149eba8f5d42a19fbe967c353}{cu\+Memcpy()}. Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory obtained with functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{malloc()}. Allocating excessive amounts of memory with cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Host() may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to allocate staging areas for data exchange between host and device.

Note all host memory allocated using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc()} will automatically be immediately accessible to all contexts on all devices which support unified addressing (as may be queried using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aadc11dd6d9f149a7bae32499f2b802c0d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED\+\_\+\+ADDRESSING}). The device pointer that may be used to access this host memory from those contexts is always equal to the returned host pointer {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pp}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d}{Unified Addressing} for additional details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pp} & -\/ Returned host pointer to page-\/locked memory \\
\hline
{\em bytesize} & -\/ Requested allocation size in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
cu\+Array3\+DCreate, cu\+Array3\+DGet\+Descriptor, cu\+Array\+Create, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga598b46f4b973520bbb04aeadaab0560d}{cu\+Array\+Destroy}, cu\+Array\+Get\+Descriptor, cu\+Mem\+Alloc, cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch, cu\+Memcpy2D, cu\+Memcpy2\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy2\+DUnaligned, cu\+Memcpy3D, cu\+Memcpy3\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoH, cu\+Memcpy\+Ato\+HAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+Dto\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoH, cu\+Memcpy\+Dto\+HAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+HtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+AAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+HtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+DAsync, cu\+Mem\+Free, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gaecabf603c2f5547fc30a15ec1135b425}{cu\+Mem\+Free\+Host}, cu\+Mem\+Get\+Address\+Range, cu\+Mem\+Get\+Info, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D8, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D16, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D32, cu\+Memset\+D8, cu\+Memset\+D16, cu\+Memset\+D32, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga9319967aebbae316ea45f540f27974b7}{cuda\+Malloc\+Host} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemAllocManaged@{cuMemAllocManaged}}
\index{cuMemAllocManaged@{cuMemAllocManaged}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemAllocManaged()}{cuMemAllocManaged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Managed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{bytesize,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocates memory that will be automatically managed by the Unified Memory system. 

Allocates {\ttfamily bytesize} bytes of managed memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. If the device doesn\textquotesingle{}t support allocating managed memory, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED} is returned. Support for managed memory can be queried using the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa2e652d7656b5e1a381b8c430e41a055e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+MEMORY}. The allocated memory is suitably aligned for any kind of variable. The memory is not cleared. If {\ttfamily bytesize} is 0, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8}{cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Managed} returns \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}. The pointer is valid on the CPU and on all GPUs in the system that support managed memory. All accesses to this pointer must obey the Unified Memory programming model.

{\ttfamily flags} specifies the default stream association for this allocation. {\ttfamily flags} must be one of \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggae58977b6b2ea67a3fb0e11949302308ea0b42aae6a29b41b734d4c0dea6c33313}{CU\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTACH\+\_\+\+GLOBAL} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggae58977b6b2ea67a3fb0e11949302308ea8b59c62cab9c7a762338e5fae92e2e9c}{CU\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTACH\+\_\+\+HOST}. If \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggae58977b6b2ea67a3fb0e11949302308ea0b42aae6a29b41b734d4c0dea6c33313}{CU\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTACH\+\_\+\+GLOBAL} is specified, then this memory is accessible from any stream on any device. If \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggae58977b6b2ea67a3fb0e11949302308ea8b59c62cab9c7a762338e5fae92e2e9c}{CU\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTACH\+\_\+\+HOST} is specified, then the allocation should not be accessed from devices that have a zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS}; an explicit call to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_t_r_e_a_m_ga52c3810ba9616e2e1dcac7247491d829}{cu\+Stream\+Attach\+Mem\+Async} will be required to enable access on such devices.

If the association is later changed via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_t_r_e_a_m_ga52c3810ba9616e2e1dcac7247491d829}{cu\+Stream\+Attach\+Mem\+Async} to a single stream, the default association as specifed during \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8}{cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Managed} is restored when that stream is destroyed. For {\bfseries{managed}} variables, the default association is always \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggae58977b6b2ea67a3fb0e11949302308ea0b42aae6a29b41b734d4c0dea6c33313}{CU\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTACH\+\_\+\+GLOBAL}. Note that destroying a stream is an asynchronous operation, and as a result, the change to default association won\textquotesingle{}t happen until all work in the stream has completed.

Memory allocated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8}{cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Managed} should be released with cu\+Mem\+Free.

Device memory oversubscription is possible for GPUs that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS}. Managed memory on such GPUs may be evicted from device memory to host memory at any time by the Unified Memory driver in order to make room for other allocations.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where all GPUs have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS}, managed memory may not be populated when this API returns and instead may be populated on access. In such systems, managed memory can migrate to any processor\textquotesingle{}s memory at any time. The Unified Memory driver will employ heuristics to maintain data locality and prevent excessive page faults to the extent possible. The application can also guide the driver about memory usage patterns via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d_ga0a8325a57b177e858b0ccdf6efd7690b}{cu\+Mem\+Advise}. The application can also explicitly migrate memory to a desired processor\textquotesingle{}s memory via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d_gaa6237bda35679c3b6b2bb6e0fe8126d3}{cu\+Mem\+Prefetch\+Async}.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where all of the GPUs have a zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS} and all the GPUs have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other, the physical storage for managed memory is created on the GPU which is active at the time \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gab3c8db1c575451d53313b05b1c6db7f8}{cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Managed} is called. All other GPUs will reference the data at reduced bandwidth via peer mappings over the PCIe bus. The Unified Memory driver does not migrate memory among such GPUs.

In a multi-\/\+GPU system where not all GPUs have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other and where the value of the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS} is zero for at least one of those GPUs, the location chosen for physical storage of managed memory is system-\/dependent.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item On Linux, the location chosen will be device memory as long as the current set of active contexts are on devices that either have peer-\/to-\/peer support with each other or have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS}. If there is an active context on a GPU that does not have a non-\/zero value for that device attribute and it does not have peer-\/to-\/peer support with the other devices that have active contexts on them, then the location for physical storage will be \textquotesingle{}zero-\/copy\textquotesingle{} or host memory. Note that this means that managed memory that is located in device memory is migrated to host memory if a new context is created on a GPU that doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute and does not support peer-\/to-\/peer with at least one of the other devices that has an active context. This in turn implies that context creation may fail if there is insufficient host memory to migrate all managed allocations.
\item On Windows, the physical storage is always created in \textquotesingle{}zero-\/copy\textquotesingle{} or host memory. All GPUs will reference the data at reduced bandwidth over the PCIe bus. In these circumstances, use of the environment variable CUDA\+\_\+\+VISIBLE\+\_\+\+DEVICES is recommended to restrict CUDA to only use those GPUs that have peer-\/to-\/peer support. Alternatively, users can also set CUDA\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ALLOC to a non-\/zero value to force the driver to always use device memory for physical storage. When this environment variable is set to a non-\/zero value, all contexts created in that process on devices that support managed memory have to be peer-\/to-\/peer compatible with each other. Context creation will fail if a context is created on a device that supports managed memory and is not peer-\/to-\/peer compatible with any of the other managed memory supporting devices on which contexts were previously created, even if those contexts have been destroyed. These environment variables are described in the CUDA programming guide under the "{}\+CUDA environment variables"{} section.
\item On ARM, managed memory is not available on discrete gpu with Drive PX-\/2.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga915327e19e4fadd40108376193e2a671}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga915327e19e4fadd40108376193e2a671} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemAllocPitch@{cuMemAllocPitch}}
\index{cuMemAllocPitch@{cuMemAllocPitch}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemAllocPitch()}{cuMemAllocPitch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Width\+In\+Bytes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{Element\+Size\+Bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocates pitched device memory. 

Allocates at least {\ttfamily Width\+In\+Bytes} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\ttfamily Height} bytes of linear memory on the device and returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dptr} a pointer to the allocated memory. The function may pad the allocation to ensure that corresponding pointers in any given row will continue to meet the alignment requirements for coalescing as the address is updated from row to row. {\ttfamily Element\+Size\+Bytes} specifies the size of the largest reads and writes that will be performed on the memory range. {\ttfamily Element\+Size\+Bytes} may be 4, 8 or 16 (since coalesced memory transactions are not possible on other data sizes). If {\ttfamily Element\+Size\+Bytes} is smaller than the actual read/write size of a kernel, the kernel will run correctly, but possibly at reduced speed. The pitch returned in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Pitch} by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() is the width in bytes of the allocation. The intended usage of pitch is as a separate parameter of the allocation, used to compute addresses within the 2D array. Given the row and column of an array element of type {\bfseries{T}}, the address is computed as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{T}}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{pElement}}\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{T}}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{BaseAddress}}\ +\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Row}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Pitch}})\ +\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Column}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


The pitch returned by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() is guaranteed to work with cu\+Memcpy2\+D() under all circumstances. For allocations of 2D arrays, it is recommended that programmers consider performing pitch allocations using cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch(). Due to alignment restrictions in the hardware, this is especially true if the application will be performing 2D memory copies between different regions of device memory (whether linear memory or CUDA arrays).

The byte alignment of the pitch returned by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() is guaranteed to match or exceed the alignment requirement for texture binding with cu\+Tex\+Ref\+Set\+Address2\+D().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dptr} & -\/ Returned device pointer \\
\hline
{\em p\+Pitch} & -\/ Returned pitch of allocation in bytes \\
\hline
{\em Width\+In\+Bytes} & -\/ Requested allocation width in bytes \\
\hline
{\em Height} & -\/ Requested allocation height in rows \\
\hline
{\em Element\+Size\+Bytes} & -\/ Size of largest reads/writes for range\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpy()}{cuMemcpy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory. 

Copies data between two pointers. {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src} are base pointers of the destination and source, respectively. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy. Note that this function infers the type of the transfer (host to host, host to device, device to device, or device to host) from the pointer values. This function is only allowed in contexts which support unified addressing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination unified virtual address space pointer \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source unified virtual address space pointer \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy2D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_c_p_y2_d__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY2D}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Copy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::src\+Host and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::src\+Array specifies the handle of the source data. \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::dst\+Host and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::dst\+Array specifies the handle of the destination data. \+::dst\+Host, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::srcY specify the base address of the source data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)srcHost+srcY*srcPitch\ +\ srcXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ srcDevice+srcY*srcPitch+srcXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::dstY specify the base address of the destination data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the base address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)dstHost+dstY*dstPitch\ +\ dstXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ dstDevice+dstY*dstPitch+dstXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes and \+::\+Height specify the width (in bytes) and height of the 2D copy being performed.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
cu\+Memcpy2\+D() returns an error if any pitch is greater than the maximum allowed (\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aac1625acc7a2db635bc1efae34030598d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PITCH}). cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() passes back pitches that always work with cu\+Memcpy2\+D(). On intra-\/device memory copies (device to device, CUDA array to device, CUDA array to CUDA array), cu\+Memcpy2\+D() may fail for pitches not computed by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch(). cu\+Memcpy2\+DUnaligned() does not have this restriction, but may run significantly slower in the cases where cu\+Memcpy2\+D() would have returned an error code.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Copies memory for 2D arrays. 

Perform a 2D memory copy according to the parameters specified in {\ttfamily p\+Copy}. The CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY2D structure is defined as\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_DEVICE}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_ARRAY}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_UNIFIED}}\ =\ 0x04}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf01ad7fe89503619b189de8776242175}{CUmemorytype}};}
