\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::src\+Host and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::src\+Array specifies the handle of the source data. \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::dst\+Host and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::dst\+Array specifies the handle of the destination data. \+::dst\+Host, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::srcY specify the base address of the source data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)srcHost+srcY*srcPitch\ +\ srcXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ srcDevice+srcY*srcPitch+srcXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::dstY specify the base address of the destination data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the base address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)dstHost+dstY*dstPitch\ +\ dstXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ dstDevice+dstY*dstPitch+dstXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes and \+::\+Height specify the width (in bytes) and height of the 2D copy being performed.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::srcY, and \+::dst\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::dstY.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
cu\+Memcpy2\+DAsync() returns an error if any pitch is greater than the maximum allowed (\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aac1625acc7a2db635bc1efae34030598d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PITCH}). cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() passes back pitches that always work with cu\+Memcpy2\+D(). On intra-\/device memory copies (device to device, CUDA array to device, CUDA array to CUDA array), cu\+Memcpy2\+DAsync() may fail for pitches not computed by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch().
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Copies memory for 2D arrays. 

Perform a 2D memory copy according to the parameters specified in {\ttfamily p\+Copy}. The CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY2D structure is defined as\+:

 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+Memory\+Type and \+::dst\+Memory\+Type specify the type of memory of the source and destination, respectively; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\+\_\+enum} is defined as\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_HOST}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_DEVICE}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_ARRAY}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_UNIFIED}}\ =\ 0x04}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf01ad7fe89503619b189de8776242175}{CUmemorytype}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::src\+Host and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::src\+Array specifies the handle of the source data. \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::dst\+Host and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the destination data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::dst\+Array specifies the handle of the destination data. \+::dst\+Host, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::srcY specify the base address of the source data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)srcHost+srcY*srcPitch\ +\ srcXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ srcDevice+srcY*srcPitch+srcXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes and \+::dstY specify the base address of the destination data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the base address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)dstHost+dstY*dstPitch\ +\ dstXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ dstDevice+dstY*dstPitch+dstXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes and \+::\+Height specify the width (in bytes) and height of the 2D copy being performed.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
cu\+Memcpy2\+D() returns an error if any pitch is greater than the maximum allowed (\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aac1625acc7a2db635bc1efae34030598d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PITCH}). cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch() passes back pitches that always work with cu\+Memcpy2\+D(). On intra-\/device memory copies (device to device, CUDA array to device, CUDA array to CUDA array), cu\+Memcpy2\+D() may fail for pitches not computed by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch(). cu\+Memcpy2\+DUnaligned() does not have this restriction, but may run significantly slower in the cases where cu\+Memcpy2\+D() would have returned an error code.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+Memory\+Type and \+::dst\+Memory\+Type specify the type of memory of the source and destination, respectively; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\+\_\+enum} is defined as\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_HOST}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_DEVICE}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_ARRAY}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_UNIFIED}}\ =\ 0x04}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf01ad7fe89503619b189de8776242175}{CUmemorytype}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height specify the (host) base address of the source data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::src\+Device, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height specify the (device) base address of the source data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::src\+Array specifies the handle of the source data. \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Device, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::dst\+Host and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the destination data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the destination data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::dst\+Array specifies the handle of the destination data. \+::dst\+Host, \+::dst\+Device, \+::dst\+Pitch and \+::dst\+Height are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, \+::srcY and \+::srcZ specify the base address of the source data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)srcHost+(srcZ*srcHeight+srcY)*srcPitch\ +\ srcXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ srcDevice+(srcZ*srcHeight+srcY)*srcPitch+srcXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dst\+XIn\+Bytes, \+::dstY and \+::dstZ specify the base address of the destination data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the base address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)dstHost+(dstZ*dstHeight+dstY)*dstPitch\ +\ dstXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ dstDevice+(dstZ*dstHeight+dstY)*dstPitch+dstXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes, \+::\+Height and \+::\+Depth specify the width (in bytes), height and depth of the 3D copy being performed.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::srcY, and \+::dst\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::dstY.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
cu\+Memcpy3\+D() returns an error if any pitch is greater than the maximum allowed (\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aac1625acc7a2db635bc1efae34030598d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PITCH}).
\end{DoxyParagraph}
The \+::src\+LOD and \+::dst\+LOD members of the CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D structure must be set to 0.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy3\+DAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_c_p_y3_d__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Copy,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory for 3D arrays. 

Perform a 3D memory copy according to the parameters specified in {\ttfamily p\+Copy}. The CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D structure is defined as\+:

 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+Memory\+Type and \+::dst\+Memory\+Type specify the type of memory of the source and destination, respectively; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\+\_\+enum} is defined as\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790}{CUmemorytype\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_HOST}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_DEVICE}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_ARRAY}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\_MEMORYTYPE\_UNIFIED}}\ =\ 0x04}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf01ad7fe89503619b189de8776242175}{CUmemorytype}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::src\+Device and \+::src\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::src\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height specify the (host) base address of the source data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::src\+Device, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height specify the (device) base address of the source data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::src\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::src\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::src\+Array specifies the handle of the source data. \+::src\+Host, \+::src\+Device, \+::src\+Pitch and \+::src\+Height are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (unified virtual address space) base address of the source data and the bytes per row to apply. \+::dst\+Array is ignored. This value may be used only if unified addressing is supported in the calling context.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7f98a88f26eec8490bfc180c5a73e101}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+HOST}, \+::dst\+Host and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (host) base address of the destination data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790aec7e15ba4b111a26adb3487023707299}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE}, \+::dst\+Device and \+::dst\+Pitch specify the (device) base address of the destination data, the bytes per row, and the height of each 2D slice of the 3D array. \+::dst\+Array is ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
If \+::dst\+Memory\+Type is \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790ad7f97cd13a156651767607456fe25b66}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY}, \+::dst\+Array specifies the handle of the destination data. \+::dst\+Host, \+::dst\+Device, \+::dst\+Pitch and \+::dst\+Height are ignored.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, \+::srcY and \+::srcZ specify the base address of the source data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)srcHost+(srcZ*srcHeight+srcY)*srcPitch\ +\ srcXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{Start}}\ =\ srcDevice+(srcZ*srcHeight+srcY)*srcPitch+srcXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dst\+XIn\+Bytes, \+::dstY and \+::dstZ specify the base address of the destination data for the copy.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For host pointers, the base address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)dstHost+(dstZ*dstHeight+dstY)*dstPitch\ +\ dstXInBytes);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For device pointers, the starting address is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{dstStart}}\ =\ dstDevice+(dstZ*dstHeight+dstY)*dstPitch+dstXInBytes;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For CUDA arrays, \+::dst\+XIn\+Bytes must be evenly divisible by the array element size.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes, \+::\+Height and \+::\+Depth specify the width (in bytes), height and depth of the 3D copy being performed.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + \+::src\+XIn\+Bytes, and \+::dst\+Pitch must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Width\+In\+Bytes + dst\+XIn\+Bytes.
\item If specified, \+::src\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::srcY, and \+::dst\+Height must be greater than or equal to \+::\+Height + \+::dstY.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
cu\+Memcpy3\+DAsync() returns an error if any pitch is greater than the maximum allowed (\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aac1625acc7a2db635bc1efae34030598d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PITCH}).
\end{DoxyParagraph}
The \+::src\+LOD and \+::dst\+LOD members of the CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D structure must be set to 0.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy3\+DPeer\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_c_p_y3_d___p_e_e_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3\+D\+\_\+\+PEER}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Copy,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyAsync()}{cuMemcpyAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory asynchronously. 

Copies data between two pointers. {\ttfamily dst} and {\ttfamily src} are base pointers of the destination and source, respectively. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy. Note that this function infers the type of the transfer (host to host, host to device, device to device, or device to host) from the pointer values. This function is only allowed in contexts which support unified addressing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination unified virtual address space pointer \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source unified virtual address space pointer \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa0fd2e63260c6317ba943af0f7e4b8d21}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+async \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memcpy
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyAtoA()}{cuMemcpyAtoA()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+AtoA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{dst\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{src\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{src\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Array to Array. 

Copies from one 1D CUDA array to another. {\ttfamily dst\+Array} and {\ttfamily src\+Array} specify the handles of the destination and source CUDA arrays for the copy, respectively. {\ttfamily dst\+Offset} and {\ttfamily src\+Offset} specify the destination and source offsets in bytes into the CUDA arrays. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} is the number of bytes to be copied. The size of the elements in the CUDA arrays need not be the same format, but the elements must be the same size; and count must be evenly divisible by that size.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Array} & -\/ Destination array \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of destination array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Array} & -\/ Source array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of source array \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyAtoD()}{cuMemcpyAtoD()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+AtoD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{src\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{src\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Array to Device. 

Copies from one 1D CUDA array to device memory. {\ttfamily dst\+Device} specifies the base pointer of the destination and must be naturally aligned with the CUDA array elements. {\ttfamily src\+Array} and {\ttfamily src\+Offset} specify the CUDA array handle and the offset in bytes into the array where the copy is to begin. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy and must be evenly divisible by the array element size.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em src\+Array} & -\/ Source array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of source array \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+sync
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyAtoH()}{cuMemcpyAtoH()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+AtoH (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst\+Host,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{src\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{src\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Array to Host. 

Copies from one 1D CUDA array to host memory. {\ttfamily dst\+Host} specifies the base pointer of the destination. {\ttfamily src\+Array} and {\ttfamily src\+Offset} specify the CUDA array handle and starting offset in bytes of the source data. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyAtoHAsync()}{cuMemcpyAtoHAsync()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+Ato\+HAsync (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst\+Host,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{src\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{src\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Array to Host. 

Copies from one 1D CUDA array to host memory. {\ttfamily dst\+Host} specifies the base pointer of the destination. {\ttfamily src\+Array} and {\ttfamily src\+Offset} specify the CUDA array handle and starting offset in bytes of the source data. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Host} & -\/ Destination pointer \\
\hline
{\em src\+Array} & -\/ Source array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of source array \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemcpyDtoA()}{cuMemcpyDtoA()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+DtoA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{dst\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{src\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Device to Array. 

Copies from device memory to a 1D CUDA array. {\ttfamily dst\+Array} and {\ttfamily dst\+Offset} specify the CUDA array handle and starting index of the destination data. {\ttfamily src\+Device} specifies the base pointer of the source. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Array} & -\/ Destination array \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of destination array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Device} & -\/ Source device pointer \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+HtoA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}}}]{dst\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src\+Host,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies memory from Host to Array. 

Copies from host memory to a 1D CUDA array. {\ttfamily dst\+Array} and {\ttfamily dst\+Offset} specify the CUDA array handle and starting offset in bytes of the destination data. {\ttfamily p\+Src} specifies the base address of the source. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Array} & -\/ Destination array \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Offset} & -\/ Offset in bytes of destination array \\
\hline
{\em src\+Host} & -\/ Source host pointer \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memcpy\+Peer\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{dst\+Context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{src\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{src\+Context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Byte\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copies device memory between two contexts asynchronously. 

Copies from device memory in one context to device memory in another context. {\ttfamily dst\+Device} is the base device pointer of the destination memory and {\ttfamily dst\+Context} is the destination context. {\ttfamily src\+Device} is the base device pointer of the source memory and {\ttfamily src\+Context} is the source pointer. {\ttfamily Byte\+Count} specifies the number of bytes to copy.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Context} & -\/ Destination context \\
\hline
{\em src\+Device} & -\/ Source device pointer \\
\hline
{\em src\+Context} & -\/ Source context \\
\hline
{\em Byte\+Count} & -\/ Size of memory copy in bytes \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemGetInfo()}{cuMemGetInfo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Get\+Info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{free,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{total }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets free and total memory. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}total} the total amount of memory available to the the current context. Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}free} the amount of memory on the device that is free according to the OS. CUDA is not guaranteed to be able to allocate all of the memory that the OS reports as free. In a multi-\/tenet situation, free estimate returned is prone to race condition where a new allocation/free done by a different process or a different thread in the same process between the time when free memory was estimated and reported, will result in deviation in free value reported and actual free memory.

The integrated GPU on Tegra shares memory with CPU and other component of the SoC. The free and total values returned by the API excludes the SWAP memory space maintained by the OS on some platforms. The OS may move some of the memory pages into swap area as the GPU or CPU allocate or access memory. See Tegra app note on how to calculate total and free memory on Tegra.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em free} & -\/ Returned free memory in bytes \\
\hline
{\em total} & -\/ Returned total memory in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemHostAlloc@{cuMemHostAlloc}}
\index{cuMemHostAlloc@{cuMemHostAlloc}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemHostAlloc()}{cuMemHostAlloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{bytesize,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocates page-\/locked host memory. 

Allocates {\ttfamily bytesize} bytes of host memory that is page-\/locked and accessible to the device. The driver tracks the virtual memory ranges allocated with this function and automatically accelerates calls to functions such as cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+D(). Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory obtained with functions such as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{malloc()}. Allocating excessive amounts of pinned memory may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to allocate staging areas for data exchange between host and device.

The {\ttfamily Flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+PORTABLE\+:} The memory returned by this call will be considered as pinned memory by all CUDA contexts, not just the one that performed the allocation.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP\+:} Maps the allocation into the CUDA address space. The device pointer to the memory may be obtained by calling cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer().
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+WRITECOMBINED\+:} Allocates the memory as write-\/combined (WC). WC memory can be transferred across the PCI Express bus more quickly on some system configurations, but cannot be read efficiently by most CPUs. WC memory is a good option for buffers that will be written by the CPU and read by the GPU via mapped pinned memory or host-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}device transfers.
\end{DoxyItemize}

All of these flags are orthogonal to one another\+: a developer may allocate memory that is portable, mapped and/or write-\/combined with no restrictions.

The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga054589ee2a0f188e664d93965d81113d}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP} flag may be specified on CUDA contexts for devices that do not support mapped pinned memory. The failure is deferred to cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() because the memory may be mapped into other CUDA contexts via the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga50f4528d46bda58b592551654a7ee0ff}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+PORTABLE} flag.

The memory allocated by this function must be freed with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gaecabf603c2f5547fc30a15ec1135b425}{cu\+Mem\+Free\+Host()}.

Note all host memory allocated using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc()} will automatically be immediately accessible to all contexts on all devices which support unified addressing (as may be queried using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aadc11dd6d9f149a7bae32499f2b802c0d}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED\+\_\+\+ADDRESSING}). Unless the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7361580951deecace15352c97a210038}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+WRITECOMBINED} is specified, the device pointer that may be used to access this host memory from those contexts is always equal to the returned host pointer {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pp}. If the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7361580951deecace15352c97a210038}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+WRITECOMBINED} is specified, then the function cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() must be used to query the device pointer, even if the context supports unified addressing. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___u_n_i_f_i_e_d}{Unified Addressing} for additional details.

{\em Flags} & -\/ Flags for allocation request\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa264c50688ed110e8476b591befe60c02}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+MEMORY} \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga9d4043c44edba509e83020336afba44d}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga9d4043c44edba509e83020336afba44d} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemHostGetDevicePointer@{cuMemHostGetDevicePointer}}
\index{cuMemHostGetDevicePointer@{cuMemHostGetDevicePointer}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemHostGetDevicePointer()}{cuMemHostGetDevicePointer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pdptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Passes back device pointer of mapped pinned memory. 

Passes back the device pointer {\ttfamily pdptr} corresponding to the mapped, pinned host buffer {\ttfamily p} allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc}.

cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() will fail if the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga054589ee2a0f188e664d93965d81113d}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP} flag was not specified at the time the memory was allocated, or if the function is called on a GPU that does not support mapped pinned memory.

For devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa904c097da7a1891f9904b3e6a49e4cdd}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CAN\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+POINTER\+\_\+\+FOR\+\_\+\+REGISTERED\+\_\+\+MEM}, the memory can also be accessed from the device using the host pointer {\ttfamily p}. The device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() may or may not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily p} and depends on the devices visible to the application. If all devices visible to the application have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() will match the original pointer {\ttfamily p}. If any device visible to the application has a zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() will not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily p}, but it will be suitable for use on all devices provided Unified Virtual Addressing is enabled. In such systems, it is valid to access the memory using either pointer on devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute. Note however that such devices should access the memory using only one of the two pointers and not both.

{\ttfamily Flags} provides for future releases. For now, it must be set to 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pdptr} & -\/ Returned device pointer \\
\hline
{\em p} & -\/ Host pointer \\
\hline
{\em Flags} & -\/ Options (must be 0)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

cu\+Array3\+DCreate, cu\+Array3\+DGet\+Descriptor, cu\+Array\+Create, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga598b46f4b973520bbb04aeadaab0560d}{cu\+Array\+Destroy}, cu\+Array\+Get\+Descriptor, cu\+Mem\+Alloc, cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Host, cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch, cu\+Memcpy2D, cu\+Memcpy2\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy2\+DUnaligned, cu\+Memcpy3D, cu\+Memcpy3\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+AtoH, cu\+Memcpy\+Ato\+HAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+Dto\+DAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+DtoH, cu\+Memcpy\+Dto\+HAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+HtoA, cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+AAsync, cu\+Memcpy\+HtoD, cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+DAsync, cu\+Mem\+Free, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gaecabf603c2f5547fc30a15ec1135b425}{cu\+Mem\+Free\+Host}, cu\+Mem\+Get\+Address\+Range, cu\+Mem\+Get\+Info, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc}, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D8, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D16, cu\+Memset\+D2\+D32, cu\+Memset\+D8, cu\+Memset\+D16, cu\+Memset\+D32, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_gac03e953b51e1011847c199286de44ac9}{cuda\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga5c85a5e76f9d425fcf2bdc71e475bdc0}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga5c85a5e76f9d425fcf2bdc71e475bdc0} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemHostGetFlags@{cuMemHostGetFlags}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemHostGetFlags()}{cuMemHostGetFlags()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Flags (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Passes back flags that were used for a pinned allocation. 

Passes back the flags {\ttfamily p\+Flags} that were specified when allocating the pinned host buffer {\ttfamily p} allocated by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc}.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga5c85a5e76f9d425fcf2bdc71e475bdc0}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Flags()} will fail if the pointer does not reside in an allocation performed by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Host() or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc()}.

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga35d83a213cb131afea32a1152539462a}\label{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_ga35d83a213cb131afea32a1152539462a} 
\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMemHostRegister@{cuMemHostRegister}}
\index{cuMemHostRegister@{cuMemHostRegister}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemHostRegister()}{cuMemHostRegister()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{bytesize,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Registers an existing host memory range for use by CUDA. 

Page-\/locks the memory range specified by {\ttfamily p} and {\ttfamily bytesize} and maps it for the device(s) as specified by {\ttfamily Flags}. This memory range also is added to the same tracking mechanism as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc} to automatically accelerate calls to functions such as cu\+Memcpy\+Hto\+D(). Since the memory can be accessed directly by the device, it can be read or written with much higher bandwidth than pageable memory that has not been registered. Page-\/locking excessive amounts of memory may degrade system performance, since it reduces the amount of memory available to the system for paging. As a result, this function is best used sparingly to register staging areas for data exchange between host and device.

This function has limited support on Mac OS X. OS 10.\+7 or higher is required.

The {\ttfamily Flags} parameter enables different options to be specified that affect the allocation, as follows.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+PORTABLE\+:} The memory returned by this call will be considered as pinned memory by all CUDA contexts, not just the one that performed the allocation.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP\+:} Maps the allocation into the CUDA address space. The device pointer to the memory may be obtained by calling cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer().
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+IOMEMORY\+:} The pointer is treated as pointing to some I/O memory space, e.\+g. the PCI Express resource of a 3rd party device.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ONLY\+:} The pointer is treated as pointing to memory that is considered read-\/only by the device. On platforms without \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa52c58d6fd1d3a72673cce199ab30cd40}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+PAGEABLE\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+USES\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+PAGE\+\_\+\+TABLES}, this flag is required in order to register memory mapped to the CPU as read-\/only. Support for the use of this flag can be queried from the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa3a3a9091a7991536d507dd5eff146d2b}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ONLY\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+REGISTER\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED}. Using this flag with a current context associated with a device that does not have this attribute set will cause cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register to error with CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED.
\end{DoxyItemize}

All of these flags are orthogonal to one another\+: a developer may page-\/lock memory that is portable or mapped with no restrictions.

The \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf1fc8645f0ab5481e7be96c80f6bfa50}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP} flag may be specified on CUDA contexts for devices that do not support mapped pinned memory. The failure is deferred to cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() because the memory may be mapped into other CUDA contexts via the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga4f20a39f0a7bddc8ce7d644327a2e7da}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+PORTABLE} flag.

For devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa904c097da7a1891f9904b3e6a49e4cdd}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CAN\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+POINTER\+\_\+\+FOR\+\_\+\+REGISTERED\+\_\+\+MEM}, the memory can also be accessed from the device using the host pointer {\ttfamily p}. The device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() may or may not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily ptr} and depends on the devices visible to the application. If all devices visible to the application have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() will match the original pointer {\ttfamily ptr}. If any device visible to the application has a zero value for the device attribute, the device pointer returned by cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() will not match the original host pointer {\ttfamily ptr}, but it will be suitable for use on all devices provided Unified Virtual Addressing is enabled. In such systems, it is valid to access the memory using either pointer on devices that have a non-\/zero value for the device attribute. Note however that such devices should access the memory using only of the two pointers and not both.

The memory page-\/locked by this function must be unregistered with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gabf51d39fdcba8462474a82c244689b1b}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Unregister()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p} & -\/ Host pointer to memory to page-\/lock \\
\hline
{\em bytesize} & -\/ Size in bytes of the address range to page-\/lock \\
\hline
{\em Flags} & -\/ Flags for allocation request\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemHostUnregister()}{cuMemHostUnregister()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mem\+Host\+Unregister (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Unregisters a memory range that was registered with cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register. 

Unmaps the memory range whose base address is specified by {\ttfamily p}, and makes it pageable again.

The base address must be the same one specified to cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p} & -\/ Host pointer to memory to unregister\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\index{cuMemsetD2D16@{cuMemsetD2D16}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemsetD2D16()}{cuMemsetD2D16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memset\+D2\+D16 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{short}}}]{us,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes device memory. 

Sets the 2D memory range of {\ttfamily Width} 16-\/bit values to the specified value {\ttfamily us}. {\ttfamily Height} specifies the number of rows to set, and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} specifies the number of bytes between each row. The {\ttfamily dst\+Device} pointer and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} offset must be two byte aligned. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Pitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination device pointer(Unused if {\ttfamily Height} is 1) \\
\hline
{\em us} & -\/ Value to set \\
\hline
{\em Width} & -\/ Width of row \\
\hline
{\em Height} & -\/ Number of rows\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMemsetD2D16Async()}{cuMemsetD2D16Async()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memset\+D2\+D16\+Async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{short}}}]{us,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets device memory. 

Sets the 2D memory range of {\ttfamily Width} 16-\/bit values to the specified value {\ttfamily us}. {\ttfamily Height} specifies the number of rows to set, and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} specifies the number of bytes between each row. The {\ttfamily dst\+Device} pointer and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} offset must be two byte aligned. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Pitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination device pointer(Unused if {\ttfamily Height} is 1) \\
\hline
{\em us} & -\/ Value to set \\
\hline
{\em Width} & -\/ Width of row \\
\hline
{\em Height} & -\/ Number of rows \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream identifier\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+null\+\_\+stream
\end{DoxyReturn}

Initializes device memory. 

Sets the 2D memory range of {\ttfamily Width} 32-\/bit values to the specified value {\ttfamily ui}. {\ttfamily Height} specifies the number of rows to set, and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} specifies the number of bytes between each row. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch().

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Memset\+D2\+D8 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dst\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{dst\+Pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{char}}}]{uc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{Height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes device memory. 

Sets the 2D memory range of {\ttfamily Width} 8-\/bit values to the specified value {\ttfamily uc}. {\ttfamily Height} specifies the number of rows to set, and {\ttfamily dst\+Pitch} specifies the number of bytes between each row. This function performs fastest when the pitch is one that has been passed back by cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Pitch().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Device} & -\/ Destination device pointer \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Pitch} & -\/ Pitch of destination device pointer(Unused if {\ttfamily Height} is 1) \\
\hline
{\em uc} & -\/ Value to set \\
\hline
{\em Width} & -\/ Width of row \\
\hline
{\em Height} & -\/ Number of rows\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa484e9af32c1e9893ff21f0e0191a12d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+memset
\end{DoxyReturn}
