\index{Memory Management@{Memory Management}!cuMipmappedArrayCreate@{cuMipmappedArrayCreate}}
\index{cuMipmappedArrayCreate@{cuMipmappedArrayCreate}!Memory Management@{Memory Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMipmappedArrayCreate()}{cuMipmappedArrayCreate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Handle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Desc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{num\+Mipmap\+Levels }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a CUDA mipmapped array. 

Creates a CUDA mipmapped array according to the CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR structure {\ttfamily p\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Desc} and returns a handle to the new CUDA mipmapped array in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Handle}. {\ttfamily num\+Mipmap\+Levels} specifies the number of mipmap levels to be allocated. This value is clamped to the range \mbox{[}1, 1 + floor(log2(max(width, height, depth)))\mbox{]}.

The CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTOR is defined as\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Depth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}}\ Format;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NumChannels;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ Flags;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y3_d___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r__st}{CUDA\_ARRAY3D\_DESCRIPTOR}};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Width}, {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} are the width, height, and depth of the CUDA array (in elements); the following types of CUDA arrays can be allocated\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A 1D mipmapped array is allocated if {\ttfamily Height} and {\ttfamily Depth} extents are both zero.
\item A 2D mipmapped array is allocated if only {\ttfamily Depth} extent is zero.
\item A 3D mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero.
\item A 1D layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if only {\ttfamily Height} is zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is set. Each layer is a 1D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A 2D layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is set. Each layer is a 2D array. The number of layers is determined by the depth extent.
\item A cubemap CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero and the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} flag is set. {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be six. A cubemap is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array, where the six layers represent the six faces of a cube. The order of the six layers in memory is the same as that listed in \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3df6d8bbf8f19ba6956c87c6b8f8eb86}{CUarray\+\_\+cubemap\+\_\+face}.
\item A cubemap layered CUDA mipmapped array is allocated if all three extents are non-\/zero, and both, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flags are set. {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be a multiple of six. A cubemap layered CUDA array is a special type of 2D layered CUDA array that consists of a collection of cubemaps. The first six layers represent the first cubemap, the next six layers form the second cubemap, and so on.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \+::\+Format specifies the format of the elements; \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\+\_\+format} is defined as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7}{CUarray\_format\_enum}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ae0af5f5a0ffa8e16a5c720364ccd5dac}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x01,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7ad0f11e851e891af6f204cf05503ba525}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x02,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a52b891ad5d4080db0fb2e23fe71614a0}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_UNSIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x03,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a376b799ee12ce9e1de0c34cfa7839284}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT8}}\ =\ 0x08,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a80864598b1579bd90fab79369072478f}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT16}}\ =\ 0x09,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a6db055c31d053bd1d5ebbaa98de2bad3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_SIGNED\_INT32}}\ =\ 0x0a,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a95c97289b540ff36334722ec745f53a3}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_HALF}}\ =\ 0x10,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaaaeb9ae979fdf3c205114a6a3128a5c7a8140f3b0de3d87bdbf26964c24840f3c}{CU\_AD\_FORMAT\_FLOAT}}\ =\ 0x20}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabb44902d50e46bbf9efbba3010c81e8c}{CUarray\_format}};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Num\+Channels} specifies the number of packed components per CUDA array element; it may be 1, 2, or 4;
\item \+::\+Flags may be set to
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} to enable creation of layered CUDA mipmapped arrays. If this flag is set, {\ttfamily Depth} specifies the number of layers, not the depth of a 3D array.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7287c43cacf1ed05865d6bcad1a23cd9}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+SURFACE\+\_\+\+LDST} to enable surface references to be bound to individual mipmap levels of the CUDA mipmapped array. If this flag is not set, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___s_u_r_f_r_e_f___d_e_p_r_e_c_a_t_e_d_ga98601aa76ddd3cedd3072207de066fc6}{cu\+Surf\+Ref\+Set\+Array} will fail when attempting to bind a mipmap level of the CUDA mipmapped array to a surface reference.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gafce9ad9aa3df839571b84b47febfb7ae}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+CUBEMAP} to enable creation of mipmapped cubemaps. If this flag is set, {\ttfamily Width} must be equal to {\ttfamily Height}, and {\ttfamily Depth} must be six. If the \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae4adf555c51852623a3dea962ab8ee85}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+LAYERED} flag is also set, then {\ttfamily Depth} must be a multiple of six.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga0c929c92a91f4d9f9f49bae0131a6ccf}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+TEXTURE\+\_\+\+GATHER} to indicate that the CUDA mipmapped array will be used for texture gather. Texture gather can only be performed on 2D CUDA mipmapped arrays.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily Width}, {\ttfamily Height} and {\ttfamily Depth} must meet certain size requirements as listed in the following table. All values are specified in elements. Note that for brevity\textquotesingle{}s sake, the full name of the device attribute is not specified. For ex., TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+MIPMAPPED\+\_\+\+WIDTH refers to the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa73cf80abc3969a6a6a9be1b9f36d7f18}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAXIMUM\+\_\+\+TEXTURE1\+D\+\_\+\+MIPMAPPED\+\_\+\+WIDTH}.

\normalsize  &
\footnotesize \{ (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+WIDTH), (1,SURFACE2\+D\+\_\+\+HEIGHT), 0 \}
\normalsize  \\\cline{1-3}

\normalsize  &

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad550651524a56766b60f10f0e7628042}{CUarray}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Level\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}}}]{h\+Mipmapped\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a mipmap level of a CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Level\+Array} a CUDA array that represents a single mipmap level of the CUDA mipmapped array {\ttfamily h\+Mipmapped\+Array}.

If {\ttfamily level} is greater than the maximum number of levels in this mipmapped array, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} is returned.

\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMipmappedArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}{cuMipmappedArrayGetMemoryRequirements()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Memory\+Requirements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memory\+Requirements,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}}}]{mipmap,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns the memory requirements of a CUDA mipmapped array in {\ttfamily memory\+Requirements} If the CUDA mipmapped array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga854c29dbc47d04a4e42863cb87487d55}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+DEFERRED\+\_\+\+MAPPING} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned.

The returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st_a19921be32de612b22f898a6fd24ebb73}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS\+::size} represents the total size of the CUDA mipmapped array. The returned value in \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___m_e_m_o_r_y___r_e_q_u_i_r_e_m_e_n_t_s__st_afc64d15c6b760c6346b2d837dd3bfe51}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+REQUIREMENTS\+::alignment} represents the alignment necessary for mapping the CUDA mipmapped ~\newline
 array.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuMipmappedArrayGetSparseProperties()}{cuMipmappedArrayGetSparseProperties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Mipmapped\+Array\+Get\+Sparse\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{sparse\+Properties,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga96db856ab3d2940fb694ce4501d9b583}{CUmipmapped\+Array}}}]{mipmap }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the layout properties of a sparse CUDA mipmapped array. 

Returns the sparse array layout properties in {\ttfamily sparse\+Properties} If the CUDA mipmapped array is not allocated with flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga8e13c9d3ef98d1f3dce95901a115abc2}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY3\+D\+\_\+\+SPARSE} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned.

For non-\/layered CUDA mipmapped arrays, \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a632ab9d5ee6722ef8e81c04a9a58dcdd}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+Size} returns the size of the mip tail region. The mip tail region includes all mip levels whose width, height or depth is less than that of the tile. For layered CUDA mipmapped arrays, if \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a4b165566317bb2212ef61b5904323e11}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::flags} contains \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga0dcf4ba7e64caa5c1aa4e88caa7f659a}{CU\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+\_\+\+SINGLE\+\_\+\+MIPTAIL}, then \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a632ab9d5ee6722ef8e81c04a9a58dcdd}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+Size} specifies the size of the mip tail of all layers combined. Otherwise, \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a632ab9d5ee6722ef8e81c04a9a58dcdd}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+Size} specifies mip tail size per layer. The returned value of \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_af3ed467c8e045c2a0c71c45154621680}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+First\+Level} is valid only if \doxylink{struct_c_u_d_a___a_r_r_a_y___s_p_a_r_s_e___p_r_o_p_e_r_t_i_e_s__st_a632ab9d5ee6722ef8e81c04a9a58dcdd}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ARRAY\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+PROPERTIES\+::miptail\+Size} is non-\/zero.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}
